<user_id>101875998493251463525<//user_id><Name>Catherine A. Montgomery</Name><Time>1574214176031</Time><rate>2< /rate>< review>
UNDER NEW MANAGEMENT. While I was taking in the art and ambience, I heard a patron ask their server about the regular menu. I didn't think much of the comment until I returned to my table and saw the menu. My travel companion and I were looking forward to tasting some of the seafood and other offerings that we found on a menu posted online when we searched for the restaurants near us.

Needless to say (see the photo of the new menu) the new owners are not offering the variety and tastes most Mexican restaurants provide. If we had wanted something like that, we would have gone to any number of chain fast food "Mexican" style restaurants in the area.

As I do not live in the area (I was visiting for an event), I have no stake in frequenting this place, but if I were in the area again, I would suggest updating the menu to accommodate the many who at one time quite enjoyed the food, drinks and music of the prior owners.

If you like Mexican fast food this might work for you, but I don't think it is a good choice, considering there are other better places - little more, but the food and service are good, too.<//review>

I was referred to Dr. Andrew Rahn by Dr. Moss of Fresno Dental Professionals...

Dr. Rahn and his amazing staff had their hands full with me. I had impacted wisdom teeth and a severe fear of surgery as I've never had any procedure done. They spent extra time consulting with me, worked with me on scheduling, and took excellent care of me. I was terrified the morning of the procedure and they were very patient with me, I actually didn't mind the procedure at all. Soooooo I've always had a DEATHLY strong fear of dentists. My fears include pain & waking up in the middle of a procedure.

<username>Jim Bass<//username><Time>1549082197259< /Time><rating>2</rating>< Review>
Let's start at the beginning of the experience.  We arrived at 6:20 and stood in line until we were able to order at 6:43.  We each ordered the Duo combo.  None of the tables had been wiped down, we found the least messy one we could and sat down for a 30 minute wait.  To be fair the cashier had warned us that our order would take 15-20 minutes.

The first of three meals arrived, the other two were a few minutes later.  The onion rings I paid extra for were cold and the sliders were right behind temperature wise.  The trays they were served on were ice cold, so that didn't help.

I ordered the Merguez and lamb patties.  I could not tell the difference between them, so I'm not sure I got what I ordered.  The sliders were good, though not as good as others like 5 Guys or Smash or...  My son ordered a regular beef patty and a chicken breast patty.  The chicken was huge and spiced with pepper.  He enjoyed the sandwich a lot.

Overall the food as just OK.  I will not be going back anytime soon though.  The wait is far too long and the food is not worth the $10/plate with that kind of wait This is not the place for a quick bite.  Though I did not purchase a beer you should expect to pay $6 on average for a glass.<//Review>

<Text>First thing's first!! Do NOT go in there thinking this is some McDonalds! The food will never take 2 minutes to come out, and I noticed many people were angry even after waiting for 10 minutes. Good news is, if you are there when the owner (James) is there, he will keep you entertained as well as the ladies who work in the front. The food is absolutely amazing and totally worth the wait. They also have beer if you're impatient and decide to relax while you wait. One of my favorite things about this restaurant is the rewards program (you earn points every single time you order there). I went there once, and then when I came back the next time, I was able to redeem $5.30 off my order but I saved my points to rack them up. I hate to see all these negative reviews on yelp and on google reviews because it sounds like people are just mostly impatient or just assuming the burgers are pre-made and warmed up for them. Try it for yourself! And when you go in, make sure you take a peak through the back window into the kitchen to see how hard these employees actually work! <userid>106802319112312462259</userid>< Text>
The food is great, wholesome sandwiches that will fill you up for moderate pricing. The smoothies are also equally good. You can get a nice deal on both if you go at their lunch special hours from 11-2pm. That being said, im rating this place 3 stars rather than 4 or 5 stars because of different issues mostly minor gripes but one big consistent problem. First the minors: the interior is very bland and unwelcoming, the tables and chairs are uncomfortable and generic, the bathroom looks like you'd go to it at a gas station in the middle of nowhere, and the service is lackluster. I would forgive these issues if it wasnt for this one thing that seems to always happen to me. I know, the suspense is killing you right now right, what could it be? Well its this, if you order big or happen to go while there are at least 2 or more people in the store then your order is very likely to be messed up or forgotten, ive had multiple times where they forgot my avocado that i generously pay for or the peanut butter in my drink or get my orders completely wrong and to only be helped about 15 minutes after. This place seems to always mess up orders or mix orders. Besides the inconsistency within the orders, the food is good, but i question why bother sometimes due to this , because, as you can imagine if you go often enough you'd get tired of not getting what you pay for. 3 stars. Average.</Text>

<review>I have been a customer of Your Basic Bird for decades. There aren't many of this exotic bird stores left,  but such stores are so much better than the big pet store chains! This store has a great selection of birds of all sizes and varieties. The owner, Claudia, is very knowledgeable about companion birds. It's clear that Claudia really cares about companion birds, and she will not sell a bird if she doesn't think it's going to a good home.If you are thinking about getting a parrot or smaller companion bird, I recommend that you talk to her. She will try to influence your decision;  she will give you facts based on her wealth of experience. The store also has a great selection of bird food;  pellets, treats, and seed mixes at competitive prices.  As well as bird cages and equipment. They offer grooming services, and twice a year Claudia hosts a travelling veterinarian who is very good. A great opportunity to get a health check up, micro chipped and groomed at a very affordable price. I highly recommend this store!< /review>< resp>

<rating>1<//rating><Review>After moving to the area, I brought my bird here for grooming a couple times and also once for boarding - I immediately felt uncomfortable when I walked in and I should have gone with my gut and found a new place right away.
The owner is the only person in the entire store who does grooming, so it's really hard to get an appointment, and the appointments that I was able to make were horrible. One time, she was 20 minutes late to my appt. So I just had to stand there in the teeny store and wait, while I was in everyone's way. Another time, she took so long doing the grooming, and held my bird so tightly that he was in extreme distress/overheated afterward. He was panting and holding his wings out and pacing - I've had my parrot for 15 years and I've never once seen him so poorly after being groomed.
The store is dirty and small and cluttered and they just do the grooming right there at the cash register. On top of that, all their parrots are tightly packed together, in relatively small cages, and they don't have a seperate space for boarded birds, so random people can just walk up and touch/mess with your parrot while they're boarded.
I knew it wasn't great, but my suspicions were confirmed yesterday when I finally found someplace else to take my bird for grooming - the other place I went was exceptionally clean and organized and open. They had an employees only boarding room (no public allowed in) and a seperate room for grooming, that looked like a proper vet room with clean tools and tables.
To top that all off, the groomer was horrified when she looked at my parrot's wings - she asked who had clipped him before, because his wings were cut waaaay too short. I felt absolutely awful knowing that I had brought him to your basic bird and allowed him to get mistreated there.

I don't know what's up with all these good reviews here - maybe people who have been coming to her for years and just don't realize how bad it is? Or people who think there aren't any other options?

Needless to say, I won't ever come back to this shop and I'm sorry that I ever gave them my business in the first place. If you're a parrot owner, please please take your baby somewhere else. Its worth the drive to go someplace with clean facilities and knowledgable, capable staff that can give your precious parrot the quality of care it deserves.<//Review>< pictures>
None</pictures>

<Text>This place is heaven for bird owners and enthusiasts.
